				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Jauchzet Gott in allen Landen, BWV 51 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1727-30? in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="27 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_voice%2C_trumpet%2C_strings%2C_continuo&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For voice, trumpet, strings, continuo</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Jauchzet Gott in allen Landen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Shout for Joy to God in all Lands
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="ja">全地よ、神に向かいて歓呼せよ</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
